towardes tremetz endamaged more waye whyche departed tybyda vntyll laste tourned selues made conflycte skyrmyssynge wyth spanyardes whyche dyd soone beate putt flyght agayne meane season departed kynge oute cytye tremetz wyth hys fyghtynge men beste treasure wyth cyty camped hyll next vnto cyty perceyued more smytten putt flyghte hasted incontinently succour wa e euen much whome came succour wanne nowe kynge departed cityethe city tremetz taken spanyardes went toke wyth theyr armye whervpon chyef ruler yet left cytye caused themperoure acceptet proclamed theyr souereygne cytye wonne tewesdaye vi daye february frenche kynge proceded lande luxeeburghethe french king duke le e pro marshial affaire hadde begonne yeare waste destroye ouerthrowe take possessyon al euer might ouercome neither resist hym sauing ye townes able abide blowe furnyshed souldiours like maner also william duke cleue land lieng maze againstethe ladye mary sendeth army againste duke cleue lady mary sister masetright beseged said army martched haste vntyll thyrde daye came sayd towne easter euen whyche xxiiii daye marche pytchynge theyr campe intendynge refreshe selues foode andthe cleueuers approche towardes brabanders reste theyr hungre paynfull iourneye sustayned duke cleue approched wyth hys armye whyche estymacyon exceded nott nombre sente sayde ladye marye infourmed waryours hadde ben amonge sayde company whyche nombre beynge espyed farre caused brabanders make alarme thynkynge none prynce orenge renatus counte nassowe hadde yere mooste parte hyndered enterpryse martyne van rossem agaynste brabante come ayde wherefore manye ran oute campe nott halfe beynge armed neuertheles brought selues battayl aray aduentures prouyde case said companye theyr frendes myghte honorablye tryumphauntly receyue yf nott myghte take lesse hurte hoost cleue approched near hys battell raye brabanders espyed whyte cross theyr banner whereby knewe assuredlye enemyes wherefore dyd also marche forwarde theyr ordre araye agaynste theyr enemyes hadde wel vewed beholden one another bothe syedes horseman bothe partyes caused theyr trompettes nflict e c eue er ders blowe theyr companye stande valyauntly vpon thys dyd also pyetons inuade one another wyth woordes whatt countre man fynde one another furth wyth rushed gether lyke valyaunte souldyours muche thatt horseman cleueners harde byckerynge soone put flyghte brabanders butt theyr pyetons defended selues muche manfullye pressed vpon brabanders suche sorte constrayened flee backwarde whan formoost beganne drawe backwardes hole hoste fled gether suche wyse theythe victory cleueners coulde nott stopped whereupon cleueners hasted smote downe euer myghte ouertake yf horseman brabanders hadde nott smytten horseman cleueners turned sayde pursuete pyetons brabanders shoulde nott one haue escaped lyue butt meanes sayde horseman myssed manye two thousande thre hundreth nexte musterynge thys conflycte gate duke cleue besydes man vnto might apeare iniury done vnto hym muche comended woulde therefore angry let hym remembre faulte hymselfe becometh historiographer story writer declare truthe thynges wherfore men vse honestie prayse shalbe walke inordinately deserue prayse actes history written ought edifye profyte come maye thereby learne ought bee eschued folowed whiche thynge without sure certayne declaracion truth done
